# 7.3.3 VIC Registers

@{Key=7.3.3; Title=VIC Registers; Body=#### 7.3.3.1 THI Registers
Refer to Reading Register Tables in the Introduction section for the register table protocol as well as recommendations for accessing registers.
- NV_PVIC_THI_INCR_SYNCPT_0
- Offset: 0x0
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: N
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xx00,0000,0000,0000,0000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
17:10 0x0 COND: 0 = IMMEDIATE 1 = OP_DONE 2 = RD_DONE 3 = REG_WR_SAFE 4 = ENGINE_IDLE 9:0 0x0 INDX: 0 = INIT
- NV_PVIC_THI_INCR_SYNCPT_CTRL_0

- VIC Registers
